./gg_H_2HDM/pythia.f:                  RVCKM=RVCKM-VCKM((IA+1)/2,(IB+1)/2)

./gg_H_2HDM/pythia.f:              RVCKM=RVCKM-VCKM((IA+1)/2,(IB+1)/2)

./gg_H_2HDM/pythia.f:              RVCKM=VINT(180+I)*PYR(0)
./gg_H_2HDM/pythia.f:                RVCKM=RVCKM-VCKM((IA+1)/2,(IB+1)/2)
./gg_H_2HDM/pythia.f:                IF(RVCKM.LE.0D0) GOTO 390
./gg_H_2HDM/pythia.f:            RCKM=VINT(180+KFOLD)*PYR(0)

./gg_H_2HDM/pythia.f:     &        VCKM(KFAOLD/2,(KFANEW+1)/2)

./gg_H_2HDM/pythia.f:     &        VCKM(KFANEW/2,(KFAOLD+1)/2)
./gg_H_2HDM/pythia.f:            IF(KFANEW.LE.6.AND.RCKM.GT.0D0) GOTO 410
./gg_H_2HDM/pythia.f:              RVCKM=VINT(180+I)*PYR(0)
./gg_H_2HDM/pythia.f:                RVCKM=RVCKM-VCKM((IA+1)/2,(IB+1)/2)
